785       error = \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689cabf350750d0d4fabd8954c0f1e9bbae94}{NO\_ERROR};
786       \textcolor{comment}{//Continue processing}
787       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
788 
789 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if (IGMP\_SUPPORT == ENABLED)}
790    \textcolor{comment}{//IGMP protocol?}
791    \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{ipv4_8h_a113cd13f7321e81a3f55491fa3b7db23a02078354528a746f693591b186db927a}{IPV4\_PROTOCOL\_IGMP}:
792       \textcolor{comment}{//Process incoming IGMP message}
793       \hyperlink{igmp_8c_a43178cad85b82edfc42b5be0b2d61817}{igmpProcessMessage}(interface, buffer, offset);
794 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if (RAW\_SOCKET\_SUPPORT == ENABLED)}
795       \textcolor{comment}{//Allow raw sockets to process IGMP messages}
796       \hyperlink{raw__socket_8c_a2c4a6c90ef9d2bf9d2c98b305d421401}{rawSocketProcessIpPacket}(interface, &pseudoHeader, buffer, offset);
797 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
798       \textcolor{comment}{//No error to report}
799       error = \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689cabf350750d0d4fabd8954c0f1e9bbae94}{NO\_ERROR};
800       \textcolor{comment}{//Continue processing}
801       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
803 
804 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if (TCP\_SUPPORT == ENABLED)}
805    \textcolor{comment}{//TCP protocol?}
806    \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{ipv4_8h_a113cd13f7321e81a3f55491fa3b7db23afef0a32d4295a591764b3e73dcf0a96d}{IPV4\_PROTOCOL\_TCP}:

809       \textcolor{comment}{//No error to report}
810       error = \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689cabf350750d0d4fabd8954c0f1e9bbae94}{NO\_ERROR};
811       \textcolor{comment}{//Continue processing}
812       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
813 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
814 
815 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if (UDP\_SUPPORT == ENABLED)}
816    \textcolor{comment}{//UDP protocol?}
817    \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{ipv4_8h_a113cd13f7321e81a3f55491fa3b7db23ab63073e81b0f3079339586add9183417}{IPV4\_PROTOCOL\_UDP}:
818       \textcolor{comment}{//Process incoming UDP datagram}

820       \textcolor{comment}{//Continue processing}
821       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
822 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
823 
824    \textcolor{comment}{//Unknown protocol?}
825    \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:
826 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if (RAW\_SOCKET\_SUPPORT == ENABLED)}
827       \textcolor{comment}{//Allow raw sockets to process IPv4 packets}

832 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
833       \textcolor{comment}{//Continue processing}
834       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
835    \}
836 
837    \textcolor{comment}{//Unreachable protocol?}
838    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(error == \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689cad80456d511d340377794c81eb5137d10}{ERROR\_PROTOCOL\_UNREACHABLE})
839    \{
840       \textcolor{comment}{//Update IP statistics}
841       \hyperlink{ipv4__misc_8c_a97921408616501cdc0795a3c4047646c}{ipv4UpdateErrorStats}(interface, error);
842 
843       \textcolor{comment}{//Send a Destination Unreachable message}
844       \hyperlink{icmp_8c_a9360e2c67e5001ebcceb50e81081901b}{icmpSendErrorMessage}(interface,

846    \}
847    \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
848    \{

      ;
856    \}
857 
858    \textcolor{comment}{//Unreachable port?}
859    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(error == \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689ca5acea867ad70b841818e19b32cc026b3}{ERROR\_PORT\_UNREACHABLE})

864    \}
865 \}
